  * No Additional Cost: You pay nothing for repairs – parts, labor, and shipping included.

#  About this item 
  * Connect & control your smart home — Easily link thousands of compatible devices from leading brands to create a connected home environment for lighting, comfort, voice assistants, energy use, and more. 
  * Automate your routines — Build custom automations using the SmartThings app to coordinate lights, sensors, switches, and other compatible devices throughout your day. Many automations now run locally for improved speed and reliability. 
  * Set up, manage, and automate devices using the SmartThings app on Android, iOS, or iPadOS. Works with popular voice assistants, including Amazon Alexa and Google Home. 
  * Easy setup with Wi-Fi or Ethernet — Set up the hub in minutes using the SmartThings app. Supports both wired Ethernet and Wi-Fi connectivity. 
  * Wide compatibility — Certified for Matter, SmartThings, Z-Wave Plus (V3 model only), Zigbee, Wi-Fi, Google Home, and Alexa. Designed for use in North America.

## Product description
###  The Works with SmartThings Smart Home Hub 
![Aeotec Smart Home Hub](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
###  Still #1. Does it Matter? You bet it does! 
This isn’t just any smart home hub—it’s the foundation of one of the world’s most trusted smart home platforms, now with support for Matter, the newest industry-standard protocol connecting devices across major brands and ecosystems. 
Built on a legacy of reliability and innovation, the original Aeotec Smart Home Hubs brings together Zigbee, Wi-Fi, Matter, and cloud-connected devices into one intuitive system powered by SmartThings. Whether you're just starting your smart home journey or expanding your setup, it gives you unmatched compatibility with thousands of connected devices—all managed by the SmartThings app by Samsung. 
Simple enough for beginners, powerful enough for enthusiasts, and designed to grow with your home. 
###  Two Hubs. One Smart Home. 
![Hub on table](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
The original Aeotec Smart Home Hub (V3) brings broad compatibility with Zigbee, Z-Wave, Wi-Fi, and Matter devices, making it ideal for established multi-protocol homes. Aeotec Smart Home Hub 2 (V4) offers next-generation speed and capability with Zigbee, Wi-Fi, and Matter support—perfect for setups that don't require Z-Wave. 
###  Simple steps to a smarter home 
![Quick Start](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
####  Super Simple Setup 
#####  3 Easy Steps 
  1. Download the SmartThings app for iOS, iPadOS or Android from 
  2. Follow the step-by-step install instructions
  3. Add your compatible smart devices


#####  Helpful Tips 
  * Start with Ethernet: Begin setup with the included Ethernet cable, then switch to WiFi in the SmartThings app if preferred
  * Check compatibility: Before adding new devices, confirm they work with SmartThings—your device manufacturer’s site is a great place to start.
  * Excluding old devices? Use the SmartThings exclusion tool to remove Z-Wave devices from previous systems before pairing them to your new hub.
  * Get inspired: Visit the SmartThings Community for tips, automations, and ideas from other smart home enthusiasts.


![Woman using phone](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
###  Control It All with the SmartThings App 
Wherever you are, whatever you connect, everything comes together in the SmartThings app. 
Create routines, build automation scenes, and coordinate devices throughout your home. Whether you’re adjusting lights at sunset, creating a bedtime environment, or setting up a morning routine, SmartThings gives you intuitive, easy-to-use controls.
Available for Android, iOS, and iPadOS, the SmartThings app makes it effortless to: ✔️ Add and manage compatible devices that use Matter, Zigbee, (and Z-Wave if using V3 model) 
✔️ Build automations in just a few taps 
✔️ Acces and Control your smart home whether you're at home or away 
✔️ Coordinate routines across multiple devices for seamless experiences 
![SmartThings Automation App](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
###  Automate Everything, Just How You Like It 
With SmartThings, you can create routines for just about anything you can imagine—from everyday moments to seasonal changes. Wake up to gradual lighting and a comfortable environment. Wind down with evening routines tailored to your preferences. Coordinate lighting, energy-saving settings, appliance behavior, and more. 
SmartThings also supports advanced home logic for power users, allowing deeper customization thanks to APIs and developer tools. 
Whether your goal is convenience, comfort, or efficiency, SmartThings helps your home run the way you want—automatically. 
![SmarThings Living Room App](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/ea7b00f9-64b2-4572-b87b-d25757e9068e.__CR0,0,900,900_PT0_SX300_V1___.png)
###  Organized by Room, Built for Real Life 
With SmartThings, your home is as organized digitally as it is physically. Devices are grouped by room, so whether you’re adjusting the lights in the living room or checking the temperature in the bedroom, everything is exactly where you’d expect it—making control fast, intuitive, and effortless. 
From the SmartThings app, you can see what’s happening in each space at a glance, manage routines room by room, and even trigger automations based on where you are. It’s smart home control that feels natural. 
![SmartThings Home App](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/6d90d703-4736-4e44-81e9-82546808e882.__CR0,0,900,900_PT0_SX300_V1___.png)
###  SmartThings for Everyday Life 
SmartThings goes beyond basic control—it offers intuitive lifestyle apps designed to make managing your home feel effortless. From keeping tabs on your laundry, to monitoring your pets, to tracking your energy usage in real time, SmartThings helps you stay on top of what matters most. 
These dedicated experiences are built right into the SmartThings app and are tailored to your routines. Want a notification when your laundry's done? Curious how much energy your home is using this week? SmartThings makes it all possible—right from your phone. 
Whether you're optimizing your energy footprint or making life with pets easier, SmartThings brings it all together in one smart, simple platform. 
![SmartThings Favorites](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/e6822ec0-c5fd-4cd6-9445-487b868ae256.__CR0,0,900,900_PT0_SX300_V1___.png)
###  Your Smart Home, Your Way 
The SmartThings app is designed to keep your most important devices and routines right at your fingertips. Pin your favorite lights, locks, scenes, or automations to your home screen so they’re always just a tap away—no digging through menus required. 
Whether it’s a go-to routine like “Good Night,” or your most-used devices like the living room lights or front door lock, SmartThings lets you customize your dashboard for fast, easy access to what matters most. 
It’s smart home control that’s not just powerful—it’s personal.

###  Maximum Compatibility. Endless Possibilities. 
![compatible devices](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
Because it’s powered by the SmartThings platform, the Aeotec Smart Home Hubs works with thousands of smart devices right out of the box. 
Both versions support Matter, Zigbee, Wi-Fi, and cloud-connected integrations, while the V3 model adds Z-Wave support. Building your smart home has never been simpler or more flexible. 
From smart lighting and voice assistants to energy-saving devices and connected appliances, SmartThings brings them all together in a single, unified experience. Works with leading brands including Philips Hue, Samsung, Ecobee, Sonos, LIFX, and many more. 
Simple enough for beginners—yet powerful enough for experienced smart home builders looking to personalize and expand their setup.

[How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void\(0\))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.
[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say
Customers find the smart hub easy to use, with the SmartThings app being particularly intuitive, and appreciate its control capabilities, with one customer noting its amazing in-depth control of smart home devices. The setup process is straightforward, with customers easily adding Z-Wave devices. However, connectivity and functionality receive mixed reviews, with some customers reporting successful pairing while others experience connection issues and performance problems. Moreover, quality and value for money are also mixed aspects, with some customers describing it as a good product while others consider it a waste of money.

_5 out of 5 stars_
##### Simple setup, tons of options
First off the setup is very simple. Download the app, run the update and you are ready to add your first device. I paired mine with some Aeotec multisensors and the only oddity found in the app shows 100% battery, and “power source” as cloud not cloud connected, even though I have the sensor wired to usb power. But all other 6 sensors show up perfectly. Lieterally hundreds of manufacturers listed for devices, so seems ill have plenty to play with, even though it’s an Aeotec product.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Compatible with LeakSmart Sensors and Water Valve ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R2NUT6OBSZDJXQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on February 17, 2024
Style: With Z-Wave - V3 - 2020[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
This is an excellent product which is very easy to set up using Samsung SmartThings app.  
  
I purchased the hub primarily for use with my LeakSmart sensors and valve. The company behind LeakSmart (not Aeotec) is out of business now. I was able to pair all the sensors and valve successfully, and configure 'Routines' easily; Those determine when the valve should close (Hint: When there is a water leak...).  
  
Some info for other LeakSmart users: In order to pair the valve, you have to remove the valve's backup batteries, disconnect the valve from AC power, then put the Aeotec Hub into pairing mode, and insert the batteries into the valve. The Hub found it immediately.  
I had a harder time pairing the sensors, but was able to pair all 4 after a few attempts. First, I put the Aeotec into pairing mode, then removed batteries from a sensor, inserted the batteries, and held the black button at the bottom of the sensor for about 2 seconds. Some of the sensors paired within 30 seconds, but with some I had to repeat the procedure several times. I am sure this is a LeakSmart thing and not Aeotec issue.  
  
I wish SmartThings offered Apple HomeKit integration, but for my particular application it wasn't an issue.  
Overall I recommend the hub.

##### [_4.0 out of 5 stars_ My Smart Home Solution ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1RTZXYAM07UUE/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on June 24, 2023
Style: With Z-Wave - V3 - 2020[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
I'm a certifiable smart home nerd (everything in my house is controllable from app or voice - all wall light switches (I use GE Enbrighten Z Wave switches), smart plugs, garage doors, thermostat, exterior door locks, blinds, appliances, security system, etc.). I had a 2nd gen Samsung SmartThings hub and decided to upgrade to the latest-greatest Aeotec version. I would have given this straight 5 stars, but very, very unfortunately, they don't have a transfer utility to move devices from an earlier version of the hub to the new one. Since I use all Z-wave devices, each one of the over 70 devices in my home had to be reset before I could connect them to the new hub. 3 of the wall switches just wouldn't reset no matter what I did so I had to replace them even though they worked fine with the old hub. Anyway, after spending a (beyond annoying) weekend methodically resetting and adding each device, we're all good to go and everything works great. The Alexa skill for SmartThings works great and Alexa picks up new devices I add instantaneously; and since SmartThings handles all of the main wireless smart home standards, you can connect just about anything to it. Plus, the SmartThings app is easy and intuitive; and I love the automations you can create (such as locking all of my exterior doors at 10 PM every night, turn on my garage outside lights at midnight and off at 5 AM every day, etc.).

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Best in breed for category - versatile and powerful without excessive tech skills ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1GUYCAG7RQR2I/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

I think that unless you want to go with the fully customizable, but you really gotta dive in, Home Assistant, or you are going with the extremely expensive managed platforms by companies that specialize in home automation and theaters, you can’t really beat this particular niche. So it’s pretty powerful, and SmartThings has a great community and if you want to learn and get very custom, you certainly can  
  
But if you want pretty powerful out of the box, along with lots of abilities, since it says Z wave, zigbee, matter, Wi-Fi… This is pretty good.  
  
I am only outgrowing it because of my desire for extreme customization on the rules side. So home assistant will be next for me.  
  
I guess my main issue is that they do not handle cameras very well nor very many of them. You can get a custom driver but I didn’t find it working very well. Right now it seems like Tapo is one of the better solutions and Aqara door doorbell video really doesn’t good job on it!  
  
But for having something that can get a lot done and is very versatile, yet doesn’t require extensive training, this is probably about as good as they get. I like it more than Apple but I still use a couple of the apple features just because I have the iPhone and iPad. I’ve got a door locked that can use NFC off of my phone. That’s a no-brainer

Race Coach
#####  _5.0 out of 5 stars_ Flexible home automation
Reviewed in Canada on July 17, 2021
Style: With Z-Wave - V3 - 2020[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
I had the 1st generation SmartThings hub and purchased this for new home. Works well and SmartThings app has come a long way in the past 3 years. In addition many of the Z-Wave devices have also improved greatly. I have used SmartThings to automate many things in my home (door locks, inside and outside lights, garage door). eg. Light inside the house by garage turns on for 10 minutes (then turns off) when the garage door opens. Light inside garage turns of when motion is detected and lights turn off automatically after 10 minutes (in case I forget). The possibilities are endless. Installing devices with the app can be frustrating and time consuming and is the hardest part. Once installed, scenes and automations are easy to create. Before purchasing an add-on device, make sure it is compatible with SmartThings and check reviews. Some work better than others.

## About this Item
  * Connect & control your smart home — Easily link thousands of compatible devices from leading brands to create a connected home environment for lighting, comfort, voice assistants, energy use, and more.
  * Automate your routines — Build custom automations using the SmartThings app to coordinate lights, sensors, switches, and other compatible devices throughout your day. Many automations now run locally for improved speed and reliability.
  * Set up, manage, and automate devices using the SmartThings app on Android, iOS, or iPadOS. Works with popular voice assistants, including Amazon Alexa and Google Home.
  * Easy setup with Wi-Fi or Ethernet — Set up the hub in minutes using the SmartThings app. Supports both wired Ethernet and Wi-Fi connectivity.
  * Wide compatibility — Certified for Matter, SmartThings, Z-Wave Plus (V3 model only), Zigbee, Wi-Fi, Google Home, and Alexa. Designed for use in North America.


## Product Description
The original Aeotec Smart Home Hub with ZWave (2020 model) is the central controller for your SmartThings-powered smart home. It connects compatible smart devices from Aeotec and many other brands, allowing you to build a unified smart home system for lighting, voice control, energy management, climate settings, and more. Using the SmartThings app, you can automate everyday routines — such as adjusting lighting at sunrise, managing energy use, or coordinating devices when leaving or arriving home. Many automations can run locally on the hub for enhanced speed and reliability, even when internet service is temporarily unavailable. The hub supports Matter, Z-Wave Plus, Zigbee, and Wi-Fi devices, offering one of the widest ranges of compatibility available. With support for popular smart home ecosystems, including Google Home and Amazon Alexa, the Aeotec Smart Home Hub helps unify your connected devices into one seamless system.
